1a1(1): / rol pa chen po thal ba'i rgyud ces bya ba bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du/ badz+ra satwa dza li su kha ma ya g+hA h+ya gar+b+ha a ba ta shasta ma hA bi na sa man ta na ma/ bod skad du/ rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ gsang ba'i snying du
1b2(1): de kho na nyid bstan pa/ rol pa chen po thal ba'i rgyud ces bya'o// bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi/ bdag nyid
1b3(1): kun tu bzang po'i gtso// sangs rgyas kun gyi dbang bskur zhing // thams cad 'dul ba'i bdag nyid kyi// rang gi dkyil 'khor rgya chen pos// phyogs bcu stong khams kun khyab
1b4(1): mdzad// rigs kyi phrin las sna tshogs pa'i// don kun dkyil 'khor chen po nyid// rang bzhin sprul pa'i bdag nyid kyi// 'khor lo gsang ba'i bdag nyid bzhugs// thabs dang
2a1(1): / shes rab rol pa'i dbyings// ma lus kun 'dus 'bras bu'i mchog/ kun nas sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // gsang sngags zab mo'i thog pa kun// yoM shes gsal
2a2(1): ba'i bdag nyid can// yon tan kun rdzogs phrin las spyod// 'di dag dkyil 'khor sna tshogs pa'i// rol pa'i kun 'jug rgyu yi gnas// tha dad min la tha dad snang // dkyil
2a3(1): 'khor kun nas sna tshogs pa'o// 'og min chos kyi grub pa'i gnas// mtha' dang dbus med 'khyil ba'i bdag/ mdzes pa'i rin chen kun gyis brgyan// tshad med ye shes 'khor
2a4(1): lo'i gnas// chos tshogs mtshan ma'i gnas 'joms shing // ma bkod ye nas brgyan pa yi// rigs kyi yon tan kun 'byung nas// yang dag tshul gyis lo tog 'joms// mya ngan
2b1(1): kun bral grong khyer che/ khang pa gru bzhi sgo khyud bcas// phyogs bcu rgya yongs ma chad pa'i// yon tan dpag tu med pa klubs// chos nyid snang ba'i bdag nyid can// ye shes nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bdag/ rang rig don
2b2(1): mthun rtags kyi tshul// rtse mo nor bu 'bar ba la// rigs kyi mtshan ma rgyan du byas// ngo bo gnyis med 'khyil ba'i bdag/ de las bsam yas grangs med pa'i// tha dad sna tshogs 'jigs pa med// de bzhin
2b3(1): nyid snang de bzhin nyid// dbyibs dang kha dog rnam dpag pa'i// rnam pa tha dad bye brag mchog khyad par yon tan gnas kyi mdzes// lha dang mi sogs tshad 'das shing // dpag med rigs kyi rgyan rnams dang //
2b4(1): kun nas sprul pa'i lha mo'i tshogs// kun nas rgya yongs ma chad pa'i// phreng ba 'chun 'phyang shar bu dag/ ye shes bkod pa ma 'dres pa'i// 'dod yon chos kyis rnam par klubs// phyogs bcu kun nas 'khrigs
2b5(1): pa yi// rang byung zhi rgyas dbang drag ldan// mtha' yas mdzad pa kun ston cing // tha dad dpag pa'i tshul gyis gnas// sgrib med gsal ba'i bdag nyid can// stong smon mtshan med 'od gsal sgo// sangs rgyas
2b6(1): theg pa rnam par spras// phyi nang gsang ba'i zab mo yi// rnam thar brgyad kyi rta babs ldan// phyi dang nang med ye shes dngos// mtha' dbus med pa'i bde chen dbyings// rgyu rkyen lam dang thabs kyi chos// de
3a1(1): / dag 'bras bu'i bdag nyid can// mi 'jigs rnam bzhi stobs bcu dang // rdzu 'phrul rkang pa dbang bcu yis// thogs med 'phyo ba lnga yi bdag/ mtshan ma rtags ni gnas rdzogs shing // thugs
3a2(1): rje byang chub sems nyid ldan// kun nas ma chags rnam par dag/ kun 'byung rin chen brtsegs pa'i khri steng na// kun tu sgrib pa med pa'i mchog/ thams cad rang gi dkyil 'khor nyid// de dag nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
3a3(1): rgyurgyan// rnam par bkod pa'i sku chen po// thams cad gsal bar byed pa'i mchog/ thams cad ma 'gags theg pa'i tshul// zab mo rgya chen gsang ba'i sngags// don kun nges par gcod pa yi// rang rig ye
3a4(1): shes 'gyur ba med// mtshan mchog sum cu rtsa gnyis dang // dpe byad brgyad cu'i bdag nyid can// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// phrin las 'jigs med snyems dang bral// chos kun spyi yi bdag nyid
3a5(1): can// nyi shu lnga yi bdag rdzogs pas// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas dag/ nyi shu rtsa lnga mngon par rdzogs// bsam gyis mi khyab thams cad du// sku dang gsung thugs bdag nyid che// A li kA li mnyam
3a6(1): gnas pa'i// zhabs gnyis pad mar bsnol ba'i rgya// brtul zhugs dkyil 'khor las kyi bdag/ kun nas thabs dang shes rab rdzogs// ye shes drug gi bdag nyid kyi// phyag rgya rin chen 'bar ba'i mtshan//
3b1(1): rdo rje rin chen 'khor lo che// dril bu pad+ma ral gri 'bar// mthing ka dkar dang dmar ba'i mdangs// rigs kyi rin chen dbu rgyan mdzes// cod pan sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag/ drug pa rigs rnams kun gyi
3b2(1): gnas// zhal gsum phyag drug mnyam pa'i zhabs// rin chen 'bar bas bde bar spras// gtso bo chos kyi mchod mnyes pa// kun bzang yum dang 'khril ba'i tshul// gnyis med byin brlabs ma 'gags pa'i//
3b3(1): gtso dang sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// rdo rje chen po thugs kyi mchog/ rigs bdag rgyal ba'i ngo bo nyid// bde gshegs 'khor lo sku yi dbyig/ zhing khams mtha' yas rgyal ba'i tshogs// yon tan rin chen che
3b4(1): gnas sbyor// de dag kun nas kun rdzogs mdzad// gsung gi pad+mo rnam par dag/ chos kyi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin// phrin las las kun mthar sbyin pas// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs mdzad// chos
3b5(1): dbyings me long mnyam pa nyid// so so kun rtogs bya ba grub// nyon mongs las kun rnam dag pa'i// rigs kyi bde gshegs thams cad mkhyen// byang chub sems nyid 'gyur ba med// ma 'dres las kun rnam
3b6(1): par dag/ yon tan sna tshogs lhun grub cing // chags pa chen po kun spyod pa// de dag phrin las sna tshogs dbyings// rang rig zhing khams chen por sbyor// phyogs bcu kun nas 'khril ba yi// 'byung ba chen po
4a1(1): rnam par dag/ gsal snang tshe gnas rnam par dag/ gsal snang rdo rje dbang phyug dbyings// sra mkhregs bde gshegs phyag rgya ste// sdud pa'i gzugs med yon tan dbyings// gsal dri smon pas
4a2(1): pad+ma'i chos// bskyed pa'i phrin las las kun rdzogs// don mthun rtags kyi phyag rgya nyid// btsun mo dam pa'i cha lugs kyis// de dag dkyil 'khor brtan par mdzad// mo yi mtshan ma'i tshogs 'joms byed//
4a3(1): der rdzogs gnyen po'i stobs dang ldan// phyogs kyi gdon rnams 'joms mdzad cing // phrin las rigs kyi ye shes rdzogs// dam pa kun dang sna tshogs pa'i// tshul rnams yang dag rdzogs pa'i lus/ khams
4a4(1): gsum che ba rnam dag cing // zag med rigs kyi dkyil 'khor nyid// til gyi gang bu ci lta bur// bar mtshams med par mtha' yas pa// byang chub sems dpa' rnam sprul pa'i// de tshe 'khor gyi byang chub
4a5(1): sems// dkyil 'khor chen po'i sogs kun nas// rdo rje bkod pa'i gar dang ni// glu gar mngon par 'khod 'gyur ba// rgyu dang 'bras bu'i bdag nyid can// smon lam thugs rje'i stobs rdzogs pa'i// dkyil
4a6(1): 'khor chen po'i gnas 'joms par// ye shes 'gro rnams rnam par dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sa chen po// kun khyab rdul bral nam mkha' nyid// thugs rje pad+mo sna tshogs ston// las kyi phrin las stobs
4b1(1): rdzogs gnon// dam shes bzhi yi bdag nyid kyis// de dag yul bcas dam par mdzad// thabs bcas ma 'dres byams pa'i stobs// sgrib med mun pa'i tshogs sel cing // kun nas spyod pa'i bzang po nyid//
4b2(1): shes rab chen po'i chos mthar phyin// gsung gi dbang po rnam dag pas// rigs kyi ye shes gsal bar sbyor// ma lus gzugs sgra dri ro'i tshogs// lha mo'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag/ de dag thams cad shes
4b3(1): rab kyis// yi ge gnas kun mnyam pa nyid// kun nas kun tu bsam yas pa'i// dus rnams lha mo'i bdag nyid do// mi mthun lha mo'i tshogs 'joms byed// der rdzogs gnyen po'i stobs dang ldan// phyogs
4b4(1): kyi gdon rnams 'joms mdzad cing // phrin las rigs kyi ye shes rdzogs// lus kyi chos kun rnam dag pa'i/ khro bo chen po'i mthu stobs ldan// rtag chad mtshan ma yul gnas rdzogs// tshad med bzhi rdzogs
4b5(1): rtogs nas sel// lcags klu zhags pa lcags sgrog dril// phyi nang dkyil 'khor brtan gnas shing // rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs mdzad// stong khams kun tu mtha' yas par// de
4b6(1): dag dkyil 'khor gsal bar snang // gnyis med mnyam pa chen po'i sku// grangs med brjod kyi mi lang bar// gnyis su med par brtan bzhugs pa'o// de nas rigs kyi sangs rgyas kun// rang gi dkyil 'khor
5a1(1): ji lta bar// mi gnyis don kun bstan mdzad de// ma 'dres stobs kyis rnam par spras// de tshe bde gshegs mthu stobs kyis// sku gsung byin rlabs mtha' yas dang // dkyil 'khor bkod pas
5a2(1): kun snang mdzad// sku gsung thugs kyi rnam 'phrul gyi// rol pa'i byin brlabs mtha' yas ston// mtha' yas med pa'i 'jig rten 'dir// ngo mtshar mtha' yas ltas kyis gang // g.yo dang g.yo ba chen po dang //
5a3(1): bskyod dang bskyod pa chen po yi// sgyu 'phrul rol pas ma lus kun// rnam dag dkyil 'khor gsang rdzogs mdzad// rigs kyi rgyal ba thams cad dang // byang chub sems rnams yi rang ste// sna tshogs mchod pa spro
5a4(1): mdzad de// yang dag don rdzogs gsol ba 'debs// sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud chen po// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i gnas// de nas mngon 'byung rdzogs byed pa'i// rgyu dang 'bras bu mtshungs pa'i rgyu// rab tu
5a5(1): / mos pas smin byed cing // thabs kyi phyag rgya gsang ba'i nyid// stong phrag brgya yi rgyud chen po// mgon po brtse ldan mtshungs pa'i lam// ma lus yum kun thabs 'di nyid// phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor bla na med//
5a6(1): khyod nyid rgyal ba kun gyi yab// dang po'i rdo rje chen po nyid// bar du mi gnas stobs rdzogs pa// bdag chen chos kyi ting nge 'dzin// phra rgyas zag med kun grol ba'i// ye shes bstan pa'i gnas 'di nyid//
5b1(1): mtshan ldan mtshan rnams kun nas rdzogs// e ma byang chub sems nyid do// de nas yul kun 'joms pa'i don// thugs rje ye shes dri ma med// thams cad thams cad las byung ba'i// byang chub sems 'di
5b2(1): rang byung gnas// mi shigs dkyil 'khor bstan pa nyid// dang po rang gi stobs rdzogs pas// ye nas yul kun rnam par dag/ thugs rje che gnas snang ba'i shugs// byin brlabs yul bcas ji ltar snang //
5b3(1): de dag rang gi las bzhin du// glo bur 'khrul pas rtogs 'dzin cing // phyi nang yul chos rnam spyod cing // thugs rje dag pas ji ltar bsgral// de dag dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs pa'i// rigs kyi gnas rnams
5b4(1): sbyor mdzad cing // phyag rgya gsang sngags stobs rdzogs pas// tshad med yul kun rdzogs pa nyid// dkyil 'khor chen po'i rnam grangs kyis// bye brag mkhas pa'i spyod yul las// rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa
5b5(1): dag/ don dam kun rdzob rnam par spyod// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba 'di// tshul bzhin dmigs par bya ba'i thabs// de ltar lhag pa'i don snang zhing // phyi rol 'byung tshogs 'gro bar bcas// sangs rgyas
5b6(1): kun gyi rang bzhin te// dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i rigs mchog nyid// shes rab chen pos yul mthar phyin// cha shas cha shas med pa yi// byang chub sems rnams drug pa'i gzungs// ma lus yul kun sbyangs
6a1(1): / mdzad cing // gnyis med ye shes chen po'i bdag/ chos kyi gnas kun rdzogs longs spyod// sprul pa'i sku rdzogs 'gro ba'i mgon// dkyil 'khor byin brlabs mngon par rdzogs// sgyu 'phrul sgrub
6a2(1): pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // lhag pa khro bo'i dkyil 'khor gyis// rang bzhin mngon par rdzogs pa'i shugs// ye shes dkyil 'khor ji lta bar// rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa dang // rtogs pas mngon par yul
6a3(1): sbyor ba'i// thun mong khyad par rigs bcas rnams// gdul bya kun gyi don bzhin du// bye brag ji ltar 'tsham par snang // 'dir ni ting nge 'dzin dag dang // ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor ma bcings pa// de
6a4(1): dag rgyu dang 'bras bu yi// tshul bzhin bstan pas rnam par spyod// 'gro ba 'dul ba'i ting 'dzin gyi// dkyil 'khor phyag rgya sngags rdzogs la/ khro bo'i dkyil 'khor mngon snang zhing // rang gi phrin las bstan
6a5(1): pa'i bdag/ tshogs sgrub ting 'dzin rgya chen po// bsod nams ye shes mngon rdzogs byed// phrin las bye brag stobs kyis ni// ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor dag spyod pa// bzhi rgyas mnyam pa chen po'i dbyings// de
6a6(1): dag phrin las ji lta bus// yang dag bya ba rdzogs par 'gyur// gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor rgya chen por// sa gzhi sa bon lha gnas rdzogs// phyogs gnas kun tu shis pa'i las// mngon par bsngags pa ji
6b1(1): lta bur// yang dag dkyil 'khor thig btab cing // yang dag tshon gong las rnams dang // phyag rgya'i bye brag kun rdzogs pa'i// rgyan chas bkod pas bla na med// dngos grub lhag ma lha gnas shing // dkyil
6b2(1): 'khor sgrub pa'i tshul dag gis// las kyi lhag chad rdzogs byed cing // mnyen shing bshes pas 'dod pa'i don// ye shes dkyil 'khor ji lta bar// dam tshig dkyil 'khor cha gnas sbyor// lha gnas sta gon
6b3(1): bum pa dang // dkyil 'khor chen po'i gnas rnams rdzogs// de nas bkra shis cho ga bzang // nye bar bsnyen pas gsang bar 'gyur// 'jug pa'i cho ga tshul bzhin du// rnam gsum nus pas mthu dang ldan//
6b4(1): bde gshegs byin brlabs brgyud pa'i lam// dad brtson shes rab ting 'dzin stobs// sbyin sreg gsang ba las rdzogs te// 'dod pa'i las kun byed par sbyor// mchod sbyin rgya chen gtor ma'i tshogs// de
6b5(1): dag yul kun rnam par 'gyur// sgyu 'phrul rgyal ba'i tshul gyis ni// lnga dang nyi shu rtsa lnga dang // sum cu rtsa lnga lnga bcu sogs// bye brag dkyil 'khor dag pa yi// cho ga kun rdzogs mngon par bsngags// sangs
6b6(1): rgyas theg pa bsam yas pa// de dag tshul rnams mtha' yas shing // sku gsung yon tan phrin las thugs// ma lus kun 'dus rnam par dag/ thabs ldan rdzogs pa'i yan lag tu// smin pa'i lam mchog bla
7a1(1): / na med// byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed cing // rang gi dam bcas sdom pa rdzogs// yul mchog khyad par 'phags pa la// byin rlabs sngags kyi nor bu blang // phan dang nus pa'i dbang thob cing //
7a2(1): rim bzhin dam tshig brtan par gnas// de dag khyad par bye brag gis// don kun gsang ba'i mngon rdzogs 'gyur// thun mong sdom pa thams cad dang // gsang ba'i dam tshig bla na med// lnga gsum nyi shu rtsa lnga
7a3(1): dang // sum brgya la sogs bye brag gis// thabs kyi theg pa rnam par spags// de dag gsang ba chen po'i chos/ khyad par dam tshig rnam pa bzhis// thams cad gnyis med mnyam pa nyid// ma lus yul kun
7a4(1): rnam dag cing // nges pa'i don rtog zab mo nyid// grogs rten mi mthun phyogs bcas pa'i/ khyad par yul kun ji lta bus// rang rig gnas rnams bgrod par byed// thun mong las rdzogs rnam spyad pa// ma
7a5(1): lus rten cing 'brel ba'i chos// thams cad tshul 'dis rdzogs byed cing // skad cig yud la lhun gyis grub// dgug dang btang dang bcings dang dgrol// gso dang gsad dang 'pham dang rgyal// gnas kyi phyag
7a6(1): / rgya kun rdzogs pas// don kun gsang ba ston par byed// bdud rtsir 'byung zhing 'gyur ba dang // bzhi brgya rtsa bzhis nad sel dag/ tshe dbang bkra shis byin rlabs ston// ma lus kun 'dus rdzogs par 'gyur//
7b1(1): thun mong rnam par bsngags pa'i chos// thams cad las 'byung stobs dang ldan// de dag gsang ba chen po'i mthus// ma lus rdzogs shing rnam par dag/ nam mkha' rdo rje sgra 'byung zhing // 'bar nas me yang
7b2(1): 'tshig pa dang // chu rgyun 'bab pa'ang de bzhin no// 'jig rten khams ni 'thor ba dang // thams cad stong zhing lhung byed pas// byin rlabs ngo mtshar yul 'byung ba// gsang sngags phyag rgya ting 'dzin stobs// de
7b3(1): dag tshul rnams kun rdzogs las// 'phags pa kun gyi gnas rdzogs pas// rigs kyi zhing khams che nas sbyor// sku dang ye shes sprul pa'i mchog/ zag pa med pa'i dngos grub kyis// don rdzogs nor bu rin
7b4(1): / chen tshul// thabs kyi bye brag tha dad pa'i// bsnyen bsgrub yan lag bzhi pas skyes// yul rnams mngon par sbyor byed pa// thog ma tha ma'i las kun dang // cho ga phun sum tshogs pa'i gnas// phyag rgya bzhi
7b5(1): yis yul sbyor zhing // rim bzhin bsgrubs pas 'bras bu'i mchog/ thams cad theg pas 'dul mdzad de// bstan pa'i gzugs brnyan bsam yas dag/ rab tu snang bas stong pa'i tshul// sgra don rgyun las snang
7b6(1): ba'o// sangs rgyas kun gyi phrin las nyid// dkyil 'khor grangs med snang ba ston// zhi rgyas dbang drag mngon spyod kyi// yul bcas mdzad pa bsam yas dag/ grangs med dpe las don bzhin spyod// de la
8a1(1): sogs te mtha' yas pa'i// phrin las kun tu ma 'gags chos// thabs mkhas sangs rgyas mdzad pa'i gnas// don mthun rnal 'byor spyod pa'i yul// bdag gzhan las kun rab tu rdzogs//
8a2(1): mnyam pa chen po'i phrin las sogs// de dag bstan pa bla med pa'i// tshul 'di rgyud chen zab mo 'di// nye bar spyod pa ji lta bur// de dag yul dang sbyar bya ba// bye brag cha shas rdzogs pa yi// don kun ston
8a3(1): pas bshad du gsol// de nas the tshom rtogs pa'i tshogs// nges par mgon pos gsal bar mdzod// byin rlabs bla na med pa'i lam// 'di nas 'jug pa'i yan lag dang // mtshan bcas mtshan ma med pa'i
8a4(1): chos// yang dag rgya chen rdzogs par ston// rnal 'byor chen po'i spyod pa dang // sa gnas lam gyi bye brag dang // bstan pa'i bsdus don ji lta bur// yang dag bka' gsol thugs rje can// kye ma thabs dang
8a5(1): shes rab spyod pa'i mthus// phyi nang dkyil 'khor rnam dag tshul chen po// rigs dang rigs bcas rnam par spyod mdzad cing // don kun gsang ba rdzogs pa'i gnas nyid yin// rab tu sbyangs pa rnams kyi nges
8a6(1): don 'di// yang dag 'bras bu'i tshul gyis rgyur bcas sbyor// mtha' yas zhing khams ye shes chen po'i gnas// kun tu bzang po'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag/ rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba gsang ba'i
8b1(1): snying po de kho na nyid rol pa chen po'i rgyud thal ba zhes bya ba las/ bstan pa'i tshul gyis rgyud byung ba'i rgyud bstan pa'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas sangs rgyas thams cad kyis rang bzhin kun tu bzang
8b2(1): po nyid/ rang gi dkyil 'khor la bzhugs shing / rang rigs kun nas longs spyod mdzad// bde gshegs kun gyis bsngags pa yi// dkyil 'khor chen po'i don 'byung ba// de dag sku gsungs thugs rnams kyi//
8b3(1): rol pa kun ston mtha' yas pa// byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kun la// tshul 'dis yang dag ston mdzad phyir// gsang sngags byin rlabs mtha' yas pa'i// ngo mtshar yul kun snang bar mdzad// mtshan nyid
8b4(1): sna tshogs kun spyod pa// de dag mtshan ma'i rgyud kyis te// mtshan ma med pa'i gnas rdzogs pas// lhan cig skyes pa'i yul rnams gsal// gnyis med mnyam pa chen po'i dbyings// byang chub sems rdzogs ye
8b5(1): shes don// skye ba med las thams cad skyes// thams cad gnyis med rdzogs pa'i dbyings// rang gi chos kun rnam dag pas// zab mo'i dkyil 'khor mtha' yas rdzogs// chos kyi sku las bzhengs mdzad de//
8b6(1): thugs rje chen po'i rnam sbrul gyis// snod bcud dkyil 'khor gsang ba'i bdag/ rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs pas// de dag don kun gsal mdzad cing // theg pa'i don 'di bka' stsal to// e ma'o/
9a1(1): thams cad rdzogs pa yi// byang chub sems nyid dkyil 'khor che// byin rlabs yul tshogs 'byung bas gnas// rig pa'i ye shes bstan pa nyid// phyogs dang phyogs las 'das pa yi// tha dad ming
9a2(1): las yul kun 'das// dus gsum kun tu mi 'gyur zhing // de dag skad cig cir mi snang // de las 'byung tshogs rnam dag cing // skye 'gro mtha' dag de nyid dbyings// yod med mtha' bzhi las 'das pa'i//
9a3(1): rgyu rkyen gnas skabs ma skyes pas// 'jig cing 'gag pa'i ngo dang bral// phyogs bcu mtha' rnams zhi ba nyid// ye nas ma bcos dben par gnas// rigs kyi rgyal po thams cad dang // snying po'i ngang du 'du
9a4(1): 'bral med// de las de byung de snang ba'i// thabs dang shes rab phyag rgya'i mchog/ srid pa gsum nyid dag pa'i zhing // snyigs ma lnga nyid bden ldan gnas// phung po lnga nyid rigs lnga'i gtso// 'byung ba'i chos
9a5(1): rnams rnam par dag/ yul kun mnyam par sbyor ba'i mthu// ma 'dres dkyil 'khor mngon sangs rgyas// thabs kyi phyag rgya rdzogs pas na// thams cad dkyil 'khor bzang po nyid// zhes rgya cher gsungs pa'o//
9a6(1): de'i tshe na zhing khams chen po'i mngon par 'phags pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i tshul gyis yang dag par gnas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rang gis btsun mo dang mnyam
9b1(1): par sbyor zhing / rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mngon par rdzogs par zhes bya ba'i tshul gyis kun tu gsal bar mdzad nas/ sangs rgyas sum cu rtsa drug gi byin gyis rlabs kyis/ rang gi gnas thams cad du gsal
9b2(1): bar mdzad do// nang gi gnas 'gro ma lus kun// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa nyid// gzugs phung rnam par snang mdzad de// tshor ba rin chen 'byung ldan yin// 'du shes snang ba mtha' yas dag/ 'du
9b3(1): byed don yod grub pa'i sku// rnam shes rdo rje mi bskyod pa// ye shes rnam pa lnga bdag nyid// byang chub sems kyi snang ba las// rang bzhin rdzogs pas gnas kun sbyor// phyi rol 'byung tshogs yul rnams kun//
9b4(1): thabs dang shes rab gnyis med par// sra brtan rdo rje pad+ma ste// gsher sdud lha mo mA ma ki/ smin byed sreg mdzad gos dkar mo// yang zhing g.yo ba sgrol ma'i mkha'o// stong gsal nam mkha' kun bzang ma//
9b5(1): rig pa thabs kyi phyag rgya ste// mtshan nyid med pa shes rab yum// gnyis med sbyor ba'i byin rlabs las// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor rgya chen po/ khams dang skye mched rnam dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpas
9b6(1): gnas kun mdzes// rang bzhin ma bcos lhun gyis grub// stong gsum 'jig rten grangs med pa'i// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas kun// kun bzang ye shes rnam bkod pas// thams cad ma 'dres
10a1(1): yongs su rdzogs// kun rdzob snang ba mtha' yas par// me long chu zla 'ja' tshon ltar// snang la ma 'gags kun ston cing // rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun gnas pa'o// kun tu bzang po'i chos rnams
10a2(1): kun// sangs rgyas bstan pas rdzogs pa nyid// de las lhag pa'i don smra ba// dmigs pa'i yul rtog kun dang bral// zhes gsungs pas zhing khams thams cad de lta bu'i ngo bor gsal bar gyur to// de nas
10a3(1): gnyis su med pa'i tshul gyis/ rang gi ngo bo ston mdzad de// ma lus mtha' yas brtags pa'i chos// ye nas dbyer med rnam par dag/ srid pa'i sdug bsngal rnam dag cing // las kyi nyon mongs thugs rje'i
10a4(1): dbyings// thabs dang shes rab 'brel ba'i dngos// thams cad yul kun rnam par sbyor// de bzhin nyid dbyings ye shes te// brtson 'grus chen po'i gnas kun rdzogs// de dag stong pa'i rang bzhin dbyings//
10a5(1): tha snyad rtog bcas rnam par dag/ gnyis med gnyis su med sbyor zhing // gdod nas ma btsal lhun gyis grub// de bzhin ye shes chen po'i sa// byang chub sems sprin rdzogs par mdzad// sangs rgyas kun gyi
10a6(1): theg pa 'di// gzhan nas btsal ba'i gnas med de// rang bzhin bde ba'i ngo bo las// mi gnas nyams su myong ba'i tshul// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rnam par thar pa chen po'i mchog/ skye 'gag
10b1(1): gnas dang dmigs pa dang // 'gro 'ong yul kun rtog bral zhing // de dag gnyis med lhun gyis grub// mnyam pa chen po'i rgyan gyis rdzogs// gsang ba'i theg pa bsam pa'o// 'di ltar snang zhing srid pa'i
10b2(1): chos// thams cad don kun rdzogs pa'i las// 'khor ba ma rig rnam rtog rgyun// sna tshogs yul bcas rtog pas bsgribs// rang bzhin bde gshegs 'dul bya ba'i// snang ba gsum gyi ngo bo la// 'khrul pa'i
10b3(1): rnam rtog 'dzin bcas pa'i// tha dad rtogs pa'i chos rnams snang // rgyu dang lam dang 'bras bu yi// bya ba chen po'i gnas rdzogs shing // bstan pa'i don kun bsdu mdzad de// gsang ba'i tshul ni bla med pa'i//
10b4(1): mtshan nyid rnam pa gsum dag gis// de dag chos kun mtshon par byed// rgyu yi chos kun mtshon par byed// rgyu yi chos kun shes pa'i yul// rkyen rnams 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid can// 'bras bu smin pas rnam
10b5(1): par grol// theg pa rim bzhin rdzogs spyad pas// rig 'dzin ye shes dngos grub cing // rab tu mi gnas mya ngan 'das// mthar phyin sa gnas lhun gyis grub// gsang ba bzhi yi mtshan nyid kyis// phyag rgya ye
10b6(1): shes mngon par sbyor// de dag yul kun gnas 'joms pas// mi mthun tshogs kyis 'jigs pa med// ye nas gsang ba chen po chos// rang bzhin gsang ba gzhir 'gyur zhing // don dam kun rdzob
11a1(1): rnam par dag/ zabs dang shes rab zung 'jug gnas// ngo bo nyid kyis lam gsang ba// shin tu gsang bas 'bras bu rdzogs// snying po gsum gyi bdag nyid kyis// don kun bsam pa gtan la
11a2(1): phebs// thams cad kun 'byung rgyu nyid las// rgyu yi theg pa bla na med// 'bras bu'i chos kun rnam dag cing // ma lus don kun bsdus pa nyid// gsang ba'i bla na med pa'i rgyud// 'bras bu'i theg pa zhes bshad
11a3(1): do// sa mchog lam rnams kun 'dus pa'i// nges pa'i phyag rgya bla na med// rgyu yi de nyid byang chub sems// rnam nyid 'brel bas kun bskyed rdzogs// 'bras bu sku mchog ye shes che// rang bzhin byin rlabs
11a4(1): thugs kyi snang // chos rnams thams cad skad cig ma// de nyid nges par gtan la 'bebs// bya ba rdzogs pa'i dus nyid du// ya mtshan pho brang dkyil 'khor rdzogs// nges don gsang ba rmad du byung // sangs
11a5(1): rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa'i yul// byin rlabs chos rnams kun gyi gzhi// 'di nyid bstan pas rdzogs par 'gyur// e ma'o bde gshegs ngo bo nyid// rang bzhin rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor las/ khams gsum
11a6(1): 'gro gnas ma rtogs pa// gnas dang der bcas thams cad dang // brtag pa'i mthu yis kun snang zhing // de nyid stobs kyis de nas 'khor// sna tshogs lus dang longs spyod tshogs// mi mthun bskal pa'i
11b1(1): tshogs rnams kyis// rgyu 'bras gnas kun so so smin// gnyis su 'dzin pas 'ching 'gyur te// rang gi rang rgyud rnam par bcings// de dag rtog pa'i gnas chen gyis// thams cad kun nas rnam par gzir//
11b2(1): yang dag bstan pa'i don rnams kyis// zabs ldan rgyud rnams grol mdzad de// bstan pa bye brag mtha' yas pas// gdul dka'i tshogs rnams grol bar 'gyur// gdul dka' kun gyi rmongs pa dang // bstan
11b3(1): pa sgron mes gsal mdzad cing // stong gsum 'jig rten mtha' yas pa// rigs bdag 'khor lo sgyur ba'i sku// kun tu bzang po'i bdag nyid kyis// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas rnams// rnam par
11b4(1): 'phrul pas kun 'gro mdzad// zhe sdang las kyis gdungs pa la// rdo rje rigs mchog mi bskyod pa// zhe sdang rgyud kun grol bar mdzad// de ltar bcom ldan thugs rje'i bdag/ don mthun bstan pas rnam par
11b5(1): 'dul// ma rig rnam rtog mun pa'i tshogs// bde gshegs 'khor lo'i tshe nas sbyor// gti mug chen pos dag mdzad de// gti mug las bcas rnam par grol// kun nas 'dod pas gdungs pa la// bde
11b6(1): gshegs pad+ma gsung gi sku// 'dod chags chen pos 'dul mdzad cing // yang dag mthar bcas sbyor bar mdzad// nga rgyal gnas kun stobs rdzogs pa'i// rin chen dkyil 'khor che nas sbyor// nga rgyal chen pos
12a1(1): yon tan mchog/ sder bcas mtha' rnams rnam par dag/ phrag dog nyid kyis 'khor ba la// de nyid rnam dag thugs rje'i mchog/ las kyi rigs mchog don grub mchog/ mtha' yas yul kun rnam par dag/
12a2(1): de la sogs pa'i nyon mongs tshogs// grangs med las kyis mnar ba las// thabs mkhas thugs rje'i dkyil 'khor nyid// mi mthun sprul pa bsam yas pa// skad cig yud la 'dul bar mdzad// ma lus
12a3(1): theg pa bsam yas kyis// ma lus 'gro rgyud rnam par sbyong // de nas sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun bsdus te// rang rig zhing khams tshogs sbyangs par// rnam par bkod pa'i
12a4(1): gnas rdzogs mdzad// bde gshegs kun tu bzang po nyid// rigs rnams bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor ni// rang gi longs spyod ji lta bar// dkyil 'khor rgya chen rnam par sprul// 'khor lo sgyur rgyal che rnams
12a5(1): dang // phyogs mtshams dkyil 'khor bkod pa'i tshogs// rdo rje 'khor lo rin chen dang // pad+ma ral gri mtha' yas pas// phyogs rnams kun tu spro mdzad cing // rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas pa// ma
12a6(1): lus 'gro ba'i don bstan mdzad// rab tu spyod pa dri med pa'i// blo gros mchog rnams 'dud par 'gyur// de dag rab dga' spangs pa'i mthus// rang gi ye shes dri ma med// dkyil 'khor 'khor lo gcig pa
12b1(1): dang // gsum dang lnga dang dgu la sogs// mtha' yas grangs med skyob pa'i sku// zhi dang drag po'i sna tshogs kyi// ngo mtshar yul kun 'bar ba bzhin// gnas skabs thugs rje chen po'i shugs// mi shes mun
12b2(1): pa'i rab rib sel// yang dag lta bas rnam par dgod// gzhan yang zhi dang rgyas pa dang // dbang dang drag po sna tshogs pa'i// rigs mchog zugs rje tshad med pa'i// mi mthun gnas kun rnam par dag/
12b3(1): 'gro ba drug po ma lus la// thub pa chen po'i sprul pa yis// thun mong khyad par gnas sbyangs te// 'dul ba rnam pa bzhi rnams dang // byang chub spyod pa mtha' yas tshogs// ma lus don kun ston pa'i sgo// de
12b4(1): sa chos kun rnam par dag/ bya ba chen po mthar phyin cing // gzhan gyi 'jug pa rab tu ston// 'di ltar 'khor ba mya ngan 'das// thams cad don kun sangs rgyas mchog/ rang bzhin rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor
12b5(1): nyid// bya ba lhun grub rnam par grol// zhes gsungs so// rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid rol pa chen po thal ba'i rgyud las/ dkyil 'khor 'brel ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o//
12b6(1): de nas 'khor gyi gtso bo'i mchog/ byang chub sems dpa' che rnams kyis// sangs rgyas kun la phyag 'tshal zhing // yang dag bstod pas mnyes par mdzad// e ma'o sangs rgyas kun tu bzang // gsang ba'i snying po
13a1(1): nges pa'i mchog/ de nyid kho na'i don rdzogs pas// sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon rdzogs pa// thog ma tha ma med pa'i dngos// ma lus kun gyi sku gsung thugs// rol pa bde ba gnas rdzogs shing //
13a2(1): byang chub mchog gi snying po'i gzhi// srid dngos zhi ba rnam par sbyong // gsang ba'i theg pa bla med mchog/ rnam gsum sprul pas bskyed par mdzod// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes sku// byin rlabs dag pa'i mdangs
13a3(1): bcas pas// shes rab dbyings dang sbyor mdzad cing // dkyil 'khor rol pas kun khyab mdzad// rgyud ces gsang ba'i don rnams kun// sbas bshad brda yis rnam par bshad// de tshe gsung dbye sna tshogs
13a4(1): pas// mig gnyis rgyud chen mtshan mar sgrogs// ji srid sbas tshig brda don rnams// thabs dang shes rab snyoms 'jug pas// e baM dbyibs kyi las bab ste// ma 'dres thams cad rdzogs pa yi// 'di zhes
13a5(1): nye bar mtshon pa ni// e sogs rnam bzhi'i dbyibs can gnas// skad ces gsang ba'i las ming can// baM zhes thig ler bcas pa yi// ma dang ma nu sdom byed yid// las can rnam shes de dag la// gsal
13a6(1): bar go bar bshad par 'dod// pa sgra don dam mnyes pa'i rgyud// theg pa chen po 'di yin no// dus ni bsam gyis mi khyab dus// de ming kun tu tshim par byed// thams cad rang rang las can gyi// dkyil 'khor
13b1(1): gsang ba mtha' yas cing // ma lus theg pa bla na med// don dam rdzogs pa'i thig le nyid// ye shes chen pos bskyed mdzad cing // las kyi rtog pa rnam par dag/ bcud 'dus thig le chen po nyid// snang dang
13b2(1): stong la sogs pa yi// brjod bya ma lus rdzogs pa'i yul// rtogs tshogs sangs rgyas lnga bcu lnga// snang bas phye phyir gnyis su med// de nas pad+ma rigs gsum pa'o// gnyis gsum brgyad kyi rnam pa can// tha ma
13b3(1): gnas dang yon tan gyis// mngon par mtho bas 'og min te// las dang bcud kyi mtha' bral bas// ye shes bzhi la dbang mi rig/ dgos pa 'byung ldan rin po che// ye shes lnga yi 'khor lo bskor// sangs
13b4(1): rgyas ngo bo bcud sdud kyis// spyi bor shin tu 'khyil bar gnas// nyungs kar sor gyis sbags par ni// sa ya bcu gsum bde bas brgyan// 'dod yon khyad par can gyis mdzes// gang yang bde byed phyi nang
13b5(1): / bral// bde ba chen po'i ngang nyid la// 'bras bu chos rnams rdzogs par snang // byang chub mchog tu nyi zla 'char// de nyid bzhugs gnas yin par gnas// dkyil 'khor kun 'byung rgya chen po// rang gi ngo
13b6(1): mtshar yul gyis 'khod// kun dang gnyis dang gnyis sbyor ba'i// cha lugs dkyil 'khor de bzhin nyid// mang po'i tshogs pa mtha' yas sgo// de dag bye brag grangs las 'das// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba
14a1(1): 'di// brtul zhugs chen po'i bdag nyid can// bcud ldan ye shes kho na'i phyir// dwangs snyigs med par kun zhugs pa// sgra dbyangs gsung gi gnas bzhi yi// dbye ba gsum gsum ngos
14a2(1): gnyis dang // bzhi bcu gnyis su 'gyur ba yin// sa ya bcu gsum la sogs par// skye gnas med pa'i ngo bo la// rten can de bzhin rten de bzhin// nyi zla thabs dang shes rab kyis// ro gnyis mnyam par
14a3(1): 'dus gsum bzhugs// dngas ma'i thig le chen po yi// bde ba dngos po ye shes snang // ma 'dres rang gi don bzhin du// sa gsum dbang phyug mchog tu 'gyur// 'dzin pa kha yi tshogs bral zhing // stong pa'i mtshan
14a4(1): ldan byang chub nyid// rab tu zhi bas grol ba yi// bcom ldan 'das ni gud na med// mtshan nyid bcom ldan bde chen po// rang gi ngo bo ma grub na// rang bzhin lhan cig skyes pa'i phyir// bcom ldan de bzhin
14a5(1): gshegs zhes bya// gzugs sogs lhag pa'i ye shes ni// las dang yon tan sngon ldan phyir// rigs kyi rgyal po nyid du brjod// bcud lnga khu ba'i thig le ni// rgyu dang las kyi kha dog lnga// ro dang las dang de
14a6(1): bzhin te// rang gi mtshan nyid kun tu snang // mkha' sogs nang gi 'byung ba dang // ye shes 'byung lnga'i las dag gis// bskyed phyir dbyings su brjod pa yin// btsun mo'i dngos por de 'dod do// thig le snod
14b1(1): kyi khyad par gyis// til gang lta bur mkha' gang ba'i// dkyil 'khor tshogs chen brjod mi lang // ma skyes mi shigs snying po can// sngon med rol mo sil snyan gar// ma lus kun 'dus rnam par dag/ gnyis
14b2(1): med thig le bcud 'dus pas// byang chub sems gnas rang bzhin nyid// mig sogs rang gi thig le ni// las dang ngo bo 'bras bu'i phyir// sems dpa' chen po nyid du brjod// nyes pa zad phyir rdo rje ste//
14b3(1): rang gi gnas kyis phye ba yis// gzugs sogs nang phyir snang ba yi// rang gi rtsa bcud bcas pa dang // bde ba skyed phyir btsun mo yin// dus rnams rlung gi go byas te// byams pa la sogs ye shes bzhi// de
14b4(1): bde rim par skye ba yang // ting 'dzin dbang du nye bar gsungs// mtha' rnams yul la zhen pa yi// ma lus chos kun rnam par dag/ thams cad yul dang dbang bcas pa// bde ba bskyed pa'i thig le ste//
14b5(1): khams gsum kun gyi gnas rdzogs pa// rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i mthus// rnam shes las 'byung dmigs pa'i tshogs// mtshan nyid rnam pa bzhi dag gis/ dga' dang rjes su dga' ba dang // dga'
14b6(1): bral lhan cig skyes pa dang // kun rdzob lugs su 'byung ba dang // don dam lugs las bzlog pa yis// yan lag nyis brgya rgyas 'gyur te// ye shes chen po'i yul mtha' phyin// mchog gi bla ma zhes bya ba//
15a1(1): tshad med bzhi gnas snyoms 'jug pa// de dag thams cad mkhyen pa yi// tshul rnams rdzogs pas brtan par 'gyur// thabs lam bde ba'i gnyer dag gis// rtag par rang gi rtog pa bzlos//
15a2(1): dngos po rnams kyi ngo bo la// bzlog bya rgyal bas mi gzigs so// thig le zung 'jug bde ba ni// sems mtha' log pas go phye nas// ye shes drug gi yul rnams su// sprul pa'i thig le rang shar ba'o// snang
15a3(1): ba mdzad pa bsam mi khyab// chags sogs nyon mongs las rtogs nas// 'dul phyir sprul pa zhes su bshad// sgra dbyangs gsung gi bstan pa la// nyes par bsgrags pa kho na nyid// phung sogs rtog pa 'jig
15a4(1): rten kun// log rtog rgyu las snang tsam las// nyi zla bden gnyis las nyid kyis// ma skyes mnyam la gnas 'gyur zhing // phung sogs lha yi dkyil 'khor du// rang snang rig pa'i mngon sum gsal// dus gsum
15a5(1): dag tu mi 'gyur zhing // theg 'di thabs kyi rdo rjer bshad// de dag yul rnams mtha' yas pas// thabs las thabs byung 'phrul pa'i tshul// ngo bo nyid kyis 'grub byed cing // yang dag spyod pas rnam par grol//
15a6(1): sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba nyid// rnam par rtog par mdor bsags shing // las kyi khams rnams dag byed pa'i// sems dang sems pa'i spyod yul nyid// snying po'i don kun rin chen 'das/ kha dog lnga yi
15b1(1): bdag nyid las// srog dang rtsol bas cher 'dzin cing // phyi nang yul kun spro bar mdzad// sangs rgyas kun gyi theg pa 'di// bde stong sbas pas mngon ston cing // grangs can bye brag gdon
15b2(1): rnams la// de dag de nyid grol byed pa'i// don mthun bstan pas bshad pa yin// snang ba rgya mtsho chen po bzhin// ma g.yos rang gi ngang las byung // de dag rim par rdzogs 'gyur te// rnam par shes ma
15b3(1): gzungs nyid do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// phyag rgya sbas pa'i tshul 'di yis// rab tu rtog bcas grol 'gyur zhing // rang bzhin ngang tshul bzang po'i gnas// rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba
15b4(1): gsang ba snying po de kho na nyid rol pa chen po thal ba'i rgyud las/ phyag rgya ye shes rjes su bzung ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas rgyal ba thams cad kyis// byin rlabs ngo mtshar bla na med//
15b5(1): kun nas mi sgrib dri med cing // yang dag ye shes chen pos grol// de tshe sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i gnas chen po// rgya chen grangs med rigs kyi tshogs// gnyis su med pa'i don gyis ni//
15b6(1): gsung gcig tshul gyis bka' stsal zhing // ngo mtshar bshad pa'i gnas la 'jug/ sprul pa'i rang bzhin 'od gsal sku// kun nas sku 'di dkyil 'khor tshogs// tshul lnga rdzogs pas 'bras bu nyid// de nyid rgyu
16a1(1): / mthun rkyen gyi gzhi// don kun gsol bas rnam dag pas// ngo mtshar yul 'di rmad du byung // chos sku longs spyod rdzogs pa dang // sprul pa rang bzhin 'od gsal sku// ngo bo nyid mchog kun gyi gzhi//
16a2(1): de dag rnam par mtshon byed pa// zab mo rgya chen sngags kyi tshogs// yi ge med dang rig pa'i srung // longs spyod rdzogs dang rdo rje dang // yan lag bsam yas tshangs pa'i dbyangs// tshul lnga thams cad don
16a3(1): brjod 'di// yang dag mchod pa'i dpal las 'das// rnam par mi rtog ye shes che// kun rdzob cir yang ma 'gags pa'i// thams cad mkhyen pa'i don kun spyod// chos dbyings me long lta bu dang // mnyam nyid
16a4(1): so sor kun tu rtogs// bya ba ye shes las chen pos// dus gsum sgrib med gsal mdzad cing // byang chub sems kyi gnas rdzogs mdzod// rnam gsum byin brlabs sbyor ba'i mthus// yon tan tshogs rnams
16a5(1): kun la spyod// zhing dang pho brang yon tan dang // longs spyod rgyan dang btsun mo'i tshogs// gdan dang rgyan cha la sogs pa// mi sgrib longs spyod rnam pa lnga// phyogs bcu kun tu ma 'gags pa// rang gi dkyil
16a6(1): 'khor rdzogs longs spyod// thabs mkhas phrin las mdzad pa yi// ma 'dres kun tu spyod pa'i tshogs// zhing dang rgyas mdzad dbang drag po// mnyam pa chen po'i lhun grub rdzogs// de dag phrin las rnam lnga yis//
16b1(1): don kun bstan pas 'dul mdzad cing // rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs pa'i// mi bzad brgyan gyi 'khor lo yi// kun nas sku gsung thugs kyi bdag/ yon tan phrin las rdzogs pa'i stobs// nyi shu lnga yi
16b2(1): bdag nyid can// rigs kyi zhing khams kun sbyor zhing // sangs rgyas thob ma bsam yas kyis// don dam spros pa chen po rdzogs// 'di ni dkyil 'khor rgya chen po// byang chub sems kyi dngos nyid las// rol
16b3(1): pa sna tshogs cir yang snang // rang bzhin ye nas ma bcos pa'i// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor mngon par rdzogs// yang dag ji bzhin rdzogs pa'i mthus// zhing khams chen po grangs med par// rin chen sna tshogs
16b4(1): bkod pa'i gnas// sa dang theg pa'i bden rnams la// rigs kyi gtso bo sangs rgyas mchog/ rnam par 'phrul nas kun 'dzem zhing // don kun bstan pas rdzogs pa'i yul// sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor mtha'
16b5(1): yas rnams// dra ba'i dkyil 'khor mtha' yas rdzogs// longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku chen pos// kun nas zhing khams chen po'i bdag/ de nas sprul pa'i sku rnams dang // mnyam rdzogs 'khrul pas 'jig rten
16b6(1): sbyong // thub pa chen po'i skyes bu mchog/ drug gi gdul bya ma lus dag thabs kyi theg pa sna tshogs kyis// kun nas phrin las rgya chen po// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje las// rang gi las bzhin rnam par ston//
17a1(1): yan lag phan tshun snrel zhi dang // spyi gtsug 'jig rten drug rnams su// bcom ldan thub sku bsam yas pas// stong gsum zhing khams gsal mdzad de// 'dul ba rnam pa bzhi dag gis// 'gro ba
17a2(1): kun gyi don rdzogs mdzad// kun nas sku yi phrin las dang // gsung thugs yon tan bsam yas pa// de dag snang ba'i sgo mtha' yas// thun mong khyad par mdzad pa'i tshogs// bcu gnyis la sogs brten par
17a3(1): bcas// mngon par shes pa'i mtha' yas pa// rab tu zhi ba ma 'dres pa'i// theg pa'i bye brag bsam yas pa'i// so so'i don bzhin mtha' yas rnams// rab tu spyod pa rnam par grol// mi dge bcu las zlog
17a4(1): byed cing // tshad med bzhir bcas bsam gtan bzhi// lha dang mi dang rdzogs pa yi// rgya tshogs kun nas ma bsgribs pa// legs bcas sdom pa bzang las 'byung // las kyi bag chags dag byed pa'o// 'khor
17a5(1): dang mya ngan 'das pa'i chos// sdug bsngal kun 'byung 'gog pa'i lam// rgyu dang 'bad pa rnam dag pa'i// rgyun zhugs lan cig 'ong ba dang / mi ldog dgra bcom brtul zhugs mchog/ rang rgyal byang chub rdzogs
17a6(1): pa'i lam// rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i chos// de nas 'khor ba'i mtha' 'gog cing // mya ngan 'das pa mngon par gnyer// ma rig 'du byed rnam shes dang // ming tshogs gzugs dang skye mched drug/ reg
17b1(1): pa tshor ba sred pa dang // len pa srid pa skye rga 'chi// chos rnams mngon par dga' ba'i mthus// 'phags pa'i ye shes zad pa'i pa med// nyon mongs las dang sdug bsngal gyi// cha shas rgyun gyi yul las 'das//
17b2(1): yang dag dgra bcom chen po'i sku// dngos med nam mkha' drangs pa'i mchog/ shes rab snying stobs las kyi mthu// sbyin dang yang dag sbyangs pa'i mthus// rnam par grol bas gzhan rgyud sel// theg pa chen
17b3(1): po'i mtshan nyid can// bdag gzhan rgyud rnams grol ba'i gros// yang dag ye shes spyod pa'i spyod// pha rol phyin pa rnam bcu yis// sa bcu ye shes rdzogs mdzad cing // byang chub phyogs kyi chos rnams dag/ ma
17b4(1): 'dres gzugs kyi spyad bya ste// yang dag theg pa'i gnas rdzogs pas// 'gro ba thams cad mgron du gnyer// tshad med bsdu ba'i dngos po yis// spyod pa rgya chen 'dzin dang bral// yang dag bsod nams ye
17b5(1): shes dag/ thams cad rdzogs pas 'bras bu nyid// rgyu yang gsang la 'bras bu'ang gsang // snying po chos kyi don las byung // sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag/ rgyud chen sgyu 'phrul dra ba nyid// phyag rgya'i dkyil
17b6(1): 'khor snang ba'i bdag/ rdo rje thig le bla med pa/ rnam dag sgyu ma'i tshul gyis ni// ma lus kun 'dus rdzogs par 'gyur// rang bzhin rnam dag de bzhin nyid// thams cad gnyis med mnyam par rgyud// zung du
18a1(1): 'jug pa mtshan nyid can// phyogs rnams gang gis brtags byas kyang // yang dag don kun dmigs dang bral// ma lus bde ba chen po'i dbyings// rang bzhin gcig tu rdzogs pa la// rnam par
18a2(1): bkod pa ci zhig 'grub// bya ba med las bya ba'i tshul// bden pa gnyis su dbyer med par// 'di dag sangs rgyas theg pa'i chos// lha mi stobs ldan la sogs kyis// rgyur bcas lam las rnam grol bas//
18a3(1): 'bras bu rig pa 'dzin pa'i mchog/ chos rnams kun gyi rgyu nyid de// de dag 'bras bu bzang po'i tshul// snying po'i don kun rdzogs pas na// ma lus kun 'dus gtan la 'bebs// ji snyed theg pa bsam yas
18a4(1): pa// de dag gsang ba snying po'i gzhi// don kun ngo bo dag pa yi// de nyid nges par rmad du byung // de ltar bstan pa sna tshogs pas// ma lus chos rnams yang dag rdzogs// rang bzhin ye shes dkyil 'khor
18a5(1): gnas/ sngon 'byung 'khrul pa'i tshul du gnas// dus gsum kun tu 'gyur med cing // yang dag mthar zug gnas rdzogs pas// dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i ngo bo nyid// zhes gsungs so// rdo rje sems dpa'i sku
18a6(1): 'phrul dra ba gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid rol pa chen po thal ba'i rgyud las/ rang bzhin dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas ting 'dzin chen po yi// dgongs pa'i don kun mnyam
18b1(1): pas na// chos rnams ji ltar gnas pa yi// ting 'dzin ye shes bstan rdzogs mdzad// de tshe 'khor gyi gtso bo dag/ rab tu gus pas gsol 'debs shing // snga ma'i don chen las byung bas// rang gi ye shes
18b2(1): 'dri bar byed// rgyal ba thams cad mkhyen pa'i gtsos// dgongs pa'i don kun mnyam rdzogs par// thugs rje chen po'i rkyen slong zhing // ma lus 'jug pa'i don bzhin bstan// phyi nang chos rnams thams cad
18b3(1): kun// sems nyid ye shes dag pa'i dngos// yul dang dbang po rnam shes dngos// phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa nyid// thams cad dngos kun rnam par dag/ byang chub sems kyi ting 'dzin ni// chos rnams
18b4(1): kun gyi rang bzhin te// de dag rang gi chos rnams kyis// sprul pa'i yul las rnam par 'das/ kha dog dbyibs sogs ma skyes par// de dag mtshan bcas dpag tu med// ting 'dzin rgyal po chen po yi// pha
18b5(1): / rol phyin mchog stobs rdzogs par// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes te// de nas chos kun lam las skyes// dngos dang 'jug pa'i mtha' bral bar// thig le mi shigs brtan pa'i dngos// rin chen sna lnga'i 'od
18b6(1): zer can/ 'byung 'jug gnas las kun skyob cing // g.yas g.yon phreng ba'i tshul bzhin bsten// lam gyi yan lag brgyad rdzogs bskyed// mkha' dbyings sprin las char gyi rgyun// glog gi phreng ba 'od dang
19a1(1): bcas// sangs rgyas theg pa bla med pa'i// bye brag can gyi tshul 'jug pa// de dag don kun rdzogs gnas pa'i// rang rig stobs skyes grol bar 'gyur// gang du dri ma med pa yi// nges pa'i mdzod
19a2(1): nas snying po las// 'od zer sna lnga'i rgyun 'jug pa// thabs kyi yan lag rnam bdun gyis// me tog phreng ba'i tshul bzhin du// bskor ba'i phyag rgya yan lag bzhi// gnyis sbyor thabs dang shes rab ste// dbyangs
19a3(1): dang gsal byed las 'phros pas/ khams gsum yi ge'i dkyil 'khor nyid// thig le rgyal po mi shigs pas// yang dag brtan pa'i ngo bor brtag/ 'od 'bar yi ge 'bru lnga yi// rang gi mtshan ma'i gnas rgyas
19a4(1): shing / khams gsum spyad pas rnam grol mdzad// sangs rgyas byang chub sems rnams kyis// thabs 'di sgyu 'phrul dag pa'i dngos// yan lag bdun gyi snang ba las// yan lag bdun gyi 'bras rdzogs 'gyur//
19a5(1): rang gi ye shes brtan byas pa'i// phyag rgya sngags kyi rgyud ldan pas// phyogs mtshams bla 'og kun gsal zhing // dkyil 'khor gnas rnams brtan par 'gyur// yang dag bsod nams ye shes tshogs// rab
19a6(1): tu sbyangs pas stobs rdzogs te// dam pa rgya chen mtha' yas pa/ khyad par sngags pa'i rgyud kyis 'jug/ phyogs rnams kun tu bkra shis pa// nye reg 'thor 'thung sngags kyi chu// rig pa'i khro bo khro mo bcas//
19b1(1): byin rlabs phyag rgya sngags kyis sbyang // thams cad rnam par dag pa nyid// mtshan bcas mtshan ma med pa'i dngos// oM mahA kro ti sho ri sarba dra byai shwa d+ha ya oM AHhUM/ rigs kyi me tog sngags dang bcas// rigs
19b2(1): kyi tsan dan bdug pa'i spos// phyogs bcur rnams par sbyor byas te// brtan par bkra shis byin rlobs 'gyur// bde gshegs kun gyi sbyor ba yis// lhag pa'i dkyil 'khor brtan byas te// sku gsung thugs
19b3(1): kyi byin brlabs dang // rigs kyi dbu brgyan mtshan bcas pas// rnam gsum sems dpa' 'khor lo yis// thams cad kun rgyud rnam par dag/ ma lus dkyil 'khor tshogs bcas pa// thugs rje sngags kyis
19b4(1): bskul mdzad pa// yang dag spyan 'dren brtan par gnas// oM AHhUM badz+ra sa ma ya swA ha/ ta thA ga ta sa man dza hUM/ thugs rje chen po'i bdag nyid kyi// dkyil 'khor kun nas brtan pa dag/ dam tshig pho brang
19b5(1): gnas pa bor// rim par gdan byas brtan par bzhugs// oM thugs rje chen po'i byin rlabs gyis// gsang ba'i theg pa bla na med// don 'di yang dag sbyor ba'i mthus// mgon po nye bar brtser dgongs
19b6(1): mdzod// e ha ya hi ba ga ban ma ha ka ru ni ka dr-i She ho/ sa ma ya s+t+waM/ rdo rje khro bo rnam spros pas// phyogs bcu'i bgegs rnams bcom mdzad de// mtshon cha me ltar 'bar ba'i tshogs// mngon par 'dod pa'i
20a1(1): gnas su spro// bskal pa'i mthar zug tshar bcad cing // ma rung ba rnams gshegs pa'i mthus// phyi yi rgya mtsho chen po mthong // rdo rje la sogs sa gzhi la// ra ba gur dang dra bar 'gyur// yang sprul
20a2(1): mtshon cha'i tshogs dang bcas// me 'od 'bar ba 'khrigs pa yi// oM badz+ra dz+wa la rat+na maN+Dal la b+h+rUM/ sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid kyi// mgon po dkyil 'khor brtan pa'i dngos// yang dag sku'i dkyil 'khor
20a3(1): nyid// mtshan ma'i 'od phreng rgyan gyis brjid// rigs gcig rigs gsum rigs lnga dang // rigs drug rigs dgu nyi shu lnga// rgya chen phyi yi nam mkha'i dbyings// rnam par snang mdzad 'khor lo mtshon// gser
20a4(1): mdog zhal gsum phyag drug pa// g.yas dkar g.yon ni dmar ba'i mdangs// 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen dang // dril bu pad+ma ral gris mtshan// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor gzhan rdzogs par// rnam gsum sems
20a5(1): dpa'i bdag nyid la// 'khor lo oM yig gsang ldan pa// gsang sngags phreng bas mdzes pa yin// bzlas brjod thig le phra mo yi// tshogs dang rigs sku spro zhing sdud// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gnas chen por//

20b1(1): lo rnam par bsgom// zhal gsum phyag dang drug pa ste// sngo dang dkar po bzhin rgyas pa// kun nas 'od zer phreng bas bklubs// sems dpa' gsum gyi bdag nyid can// gsang sngags phreng bas 'khrigs pa
20b2(1): yi// 'od 'phro 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor nyid// gcig dang gsum la sogs pa'i bdag/ lhag par mos pa'i gnas bsgom ste// pad+ma a yig mtshan ldan par// thabs dang shes rab phreng ba'i gnas// dbang po
20b3(1): thig le rdzogs pa nyid// 'od phreng sngags kyi rnam pa yis// phra mo rdzogs pa'i bar du bsgom// gnyis med ye shes rnam grol bas// gsung gi dkyil 'khor brtan par 'gyur// thugs mchog rdo rje sems dpa'

21a1(1): bo nyid// zhal gsum phyag drug rgyan gyis mdzes// sngo dang dkar dang dmar ba'i 'od// rin chen la sogs mtshan mas brgyan// sems dpa' gsum gyi bdag nyid can// rin chen gnas 'bar sa

23b2(1): mchog/ thig le chen po mnyam ldan pas// byang chub yan lag rnam par 'phro// tshul rnams bgrod pa med pa'i lam// thabs dang shes rab rgyas pa yi// rdo rje rnam bzhi dag pa'i tshul// rab tu sbyangs pas sangs
23b3(1): rgyas mchog/ de ltar bsnyen pa'i dkyil 'khor gyis// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor che gnas sbyor// sangs rgyas kun dang gcig pa'i blos// nye bar bsnyen pa'i rgyun ldan zhing // byang chub sems kyi yi ge nyid// rang
23b4(1): gi gnas su rdzogs byed pa'o// de dag goms par gsal ba dang // mi shigs thig le brtan par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gsung thugs// thabs rnams sgrub pa'i phyag rgya nyid// mngon sum rigs kyi sku
23b5(1): sbyor zhing // sa gzhi khyad par sbyor mdzad pas// rdzu 'phrul theg pa gzhan rgyud sel// yang dag sgrub pa chen po'i mchog/ rtags kyi phyag rgya gnyis med tshul/ khams gsum gnas rnams rdzogs byed pa'i// phyag
23b6(1): rgya chen po'i rigs kyi bdag/ theg pa'i mtha' rnams ma 'gags par// kun 'byung gnas kyi cho 'phrul nyid// yid bzhin nor bu rin chen mchog/ phyogs bcu kun nas bsngags pa'o// rgyal ba kun gyi gnas
24a1(1): rdzogs pa'i// sna rtse'i thig le rin chen lnga// dbang po drug gi yul dang ldan// yan lag grangs dang bgrang 'das par// mtshan ma rnam pa bzhi ldan zhing // ji srid brtan pa'i gnas su gzhag/ byang
24a2(1): chub sems kun rdzogs pas na// bcu drug cha shas grangs las 'das// mi ldog gnas kyi ting nge 'dzin// nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor kha sbyar ba'o// rim bzhin dbang po drug gi yul// sgro dang bsdu ba'i yan
24a3(1): lag gis// gsang sngags phyag rgya kun rdzogs par// rigs gcig gsum dang lnga la sogs// thabs kyi yan lag bsam yas zhing // zhing khams gnas kun dag par byed// rdo rje 'khor lo rin chen dang //
24a4(1): pad+mo mtshan bcas ral grir bcas// 'od zer sna lnga'i phreng ba nyid// kun nas 'khrigs pas sngags dang bcas// gsang gsum dam tshig ye shes che/ kha sbyor thig le la rdzogs pa'i// phyag rgya gsang ba'i yi ge/
24a5(1): mchog/ bdun 'gyur drag po'i gsang tshig bcas// ma ni gnas las grol ba yis// rang gi phyag rgya thams cad pas// rin chen ga'u'i bcud rdzogs te// nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor dbab par 'gyur// gnas dang
24a6(1): gnas min gsang ba'i yul// phra mo sems kyi ting 'dzin gyis// tha snyad thams cad 'gog byed cing / khams gsum skye 'gro rnam par dag/ yang dag 'brel pas rnam par dag/ yang dag 'brel pas goms pa
24b1(1): dang // brda' yi ming tshig sum cu gnyis// thig le 'od zer sna tshogs dang // rab tu zhugs pas bde chen dbyings// ji srid brtan par gnas pa'i dus// kun 'dzin yi ge sdom byed cing // dbab dang bsgril
24b2(1): dang spro ba dang // slar bsdu yang dag ye shes gnas// thabs dang shes rab snyoms zhugs rnams// nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bye brag rdzogs// don kun gsang ba'i de bzhin nyid// byams pa chen pos gzhan rgyud sel//
24b3(1): gcig pur rus sbrul skam sogs bzhin// gnyis med 'khril ba'i cha lugs dag/ gnas mthar dbang pos gzhan du bskur// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor rang nyid kyis// phyag rgya bde ba mtshan ma bcas// nyon
24b4(1): ngas gnas kun grol byed pa// sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad ye shes nyid// dngos po sangs rgyas bzang po la// rigs rnams rdzogs pas dbu brgyan cing // thugs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par bkod// me rlung sbyor bas
24b5(1): bskyal byas te// thig le 'od zer gyen 'bar bas// smin byed khyab par bde ba'i mchog/ rang gi gnas su rnam par 'khril// sprul pa'i 'khor lo cha rgyas pa// 'od 'bar chags pa'i ri mo can// oM yig sngags
24b6(1): kyi phreng bas mdzes// drug cu rtsa lnga gnas rnams su// bde chen thig le'i tshul bzhugs shing // de ming bde ba'i sgra dang bcas// thabs kyi tshul ni rnam par dbab// chos kyi 'khor lo hUM yig rdzogs// dkar
25a1(1): / ser 'od zer sna lnga'i mdangs// gnas brgyad yi ge'i phreng bas mdzes// shes rab brgyad gnas ye shes rdzogs// byams pa chen po'i don kun ston// de dag skye dang 'gag pa dang // yang dag
25a2(1): skraspangs pas kun grol zhing // gnyis med ye shes rton pa'i tshul// sgra rnams brjod pa'i tshul 'das pas// gsang gsum dam tshig sngags kyi gnas// bcu drug bdud rtsi 'dzag pa yi// dkar dmar 'od zer phreng
25a3(1): ba can// oM yig sngags kyi yi ges brgyan// kun 'byung rdzogs pa'i yi ge ste// spro dang bsdu ba dag gi tshul// mi 'gyur brtan pa'i thig le nyid// haM yig sngon po byang chub sems// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la
25a4(1): gnas shing // kun da dung gi 'od gsal mdangs// sum cu rtsa gnyis yi ge'i tshogs// 'khor lo'i gnas la snyoms 'jug cing // rang gi dkyil 'khor brtan byed pa'o// dga' dang rjes su dga' ba dang //
25a5(1): dga' bral lhan cig skyes pa yi// yan lag cha shas kun rdzogs pa'o// gnas skabs chos kyi bye brag gis// dngos grub phrin las brtan byed cing // 'dod pa'i yul kun rnam par sbyor/ tha dad tshogs rnams
25a6(1): dag pa yi// ye shes bcu drug rim gyis rdzogs// g.yas dang g.yon gyi sbyor ba las// A li kA li'i gnas rdzogs te// nyi zla'i 'od zer spro ba dang // rab tu goms pas dkyil 'khor rdzogs// bde chen sdig
25b1(1): bral gzungs su gnas// mtshan nyid ji bzhin tshul 'jug pas// phyag rgya'i thig le'i 'bebs par byed// nyi dkyil rdo rje la gnas pa'i// hUM yig 'od 'bar rin po che// cha shas rdzogs pa'i sku yi dbyig/ snying
25b2(1): po sa bon gsang bas mtshan// pad+ma a yig las byung ba'i// gru gsum chos kyi b+ha ga bzang // ge sar ze 'bru'i snying po can// rten 'brel ho yig mdzes par gnas// g.yas dang g.yon gyi sbyor ba las// ma
25b3(1): lus chags pa chen po'i dngos// dam tshig chags pa'i brdas bskul zhing // phyag rgya bzhi yis snyoms 'jug pas// yang dag ye shes rdzogs par sbyor// nyi zla dus gcig 'char ba yi// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor
25b4(1): gsal bar rdzogs// sangs rgyas thams cad mchod byed cing // yang dag rdzogs pa'i gnyis su med// 'gro rnams rgya chen ma lus dag/ dbang bskur rnam par dag pa'i mthus// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor rgyas pa
25b5(1): nyid// rnal 'byor chen po gsal bar mdzad// pho brang bdun bcas yang dag rdzogs// shes rab thabs ni phyag rgya las// rigs rnams dkyil 'khor brtan gnas shing // cho ga rnam pa gsum dag gis// thar
25b6(1): pa chen po'i grong khyer mchog/ rang bzhin rigs mchog lhun gyis grub// phyi rol 'gro ba'i gnas spros te// zhing khams chen po rnam par dag rigs kyi bdag po de nyid bzhin// 'bras bu rdzogs pas dkyil
26a1(1): / 'khor che// thams cad gcig tu bsdus pa yi// cho ga rdo rje brtan pa'i bdag/ gsal byed oM yig las 'phros pa// sna tshogs sku yi dkyil 'khor rnams// bde bshegs kun gyis gnas 'jug cing //
26a2(1): rigs kyi sku gnas rdzogs par mdzad// rnam dag pad+ma'i 'od zer gyis// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba mnyes mdzad cing // byang chub sems tshogs rnams bsdus te// gsang ba'i phyag rgya dkyil 'khor nyid// 'dod
26a3(1): tshogs gsung gi dkyil 'khor las// thugs rje'i nyi ma rnam par 'phro// rig pa'i dngos grub bzang po dag/ byang chub sems kyi brtan par byed// gnas lnga'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa las// mtshan ma lags
26a4(1): so 'od bcas la// ming gnyis brtan pa'i sngags kyis brgyan// rigs lnga'i dam tshig brtan par 'gyur// byin rlabs kun nas rdzogs pa yi// ye shes lnga yi don mtshon cing // rnam par grol bas brtan byed pa//
26a5(1): de dag sangs rgyas theg pa'i mchog/ rang nyid chos kyis rdzogs par 'gyur// ji srid dkyil 'khor rnam gnyis dag/ phyogs kyi cha shas rnam phye ste// bye brag yul kun sbyor byed pas// rnam par grol ba'i dngos
26a6(1): grub nyid// ting 'dzin rnam pa lnga dag gis// sangs rgyas kun gyi yul bcas sbyor// dbang bskur byin brlabs rdzogs byas te// rigs kyi bdag pos nye bar mdzes// thun mong bzlas pa'i yan lag nyid//
26b1(1): dkyil 'khor kun tu byin brlabs pa'i// de dag sems dpa' gsum gyi mdzes// yi ge dpa' bo 'bru lnga'i sngags// 'od bcas 'khor lo'i rnam pa bzhin// ji srid mtshan ma'i rtags ldan par// sku gsung
26b2(1): thugs kyi phyag rgya'i gzung // brtan par ma 'gyur mi gtang zhing // gsal zhing rdzogs pas kun tu spro// ji ltar 'dod pa'i yul rnams kun// cho ga 'di yi rdzogs par 'gyur// de dag lha rnams kun gyi gnas//
26b3(1): rab tu rdzogs pa'i 'khor lo'i tshul// gsang sngags rgyal po phreng ba'i bdag/ gnas gsum phyag rgya'i gnas rdzogs par// myur dang bul ba la sogs spangs// don bzhin brtsams pas dngos grub mchog/ rang
26b4(1): gi lhag pa'i lha gnas dag/ yang dag sbyor bas bstan pa nyid// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje'i mchog/ yon tan phrin las gnas rgyas par// phyag rgya bzang po gnas lnga la// sa bon sngags ni phreng bas brgyan//
26b5(1): rigs lnga'i bzlas brjod brtson ldan pas// rigs bsam gcig par rdzogs byas te// nor bu gang bar gyur pa dag/ pad+ma'i gnas su yang dag spro// spyi gtsug la sogs gnas lnga dag/ 'khor lo phreng ba ji
26b6(1): bzhin par// yang dang yang du sbyor ba bya// las kun dang po las sbyor ba// dang po'i sems tsam spyad pa ste// dang po'i mtshan ma rdzogs kyi bar// yang dang yang du bslab par bya// rim gyi ye shes las sbyar te//
27a1(1): ci zhig dbang dang yang dag dbang // shin tu rnam par grol ba'i mthus// rang gi bsam gtan las spyad cing // yul grogs rten gyi bye brag kun// rim gyis sbyor ba'i stobs kyis gsal// mtshon
27a2(1): pa'i bzlas pa sna tshogs dag/ mtshan bcas rgyud kyi rim bzhin te// yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu// thams cad gnyis med sbyor bas grol// de dag cha shas las 'das pa'i// ming gnyis bstan pa'i ting nge
27a3(1): 'dzin// 'byung 'jug gnas pa'i rtsol ba las// rin chen sna lnga'i phreng ba dag/ 'khor lo rgyun gyi mnyam rdzogs pas// lnga dang bcu dang nyi shu dang // nyi shu rtsa lnga sum cu sogs// nyi khri tshig stong bye ba'i bar//
27a4(1): grangs ldan grangs las 'das pa yi// cha shas thig le mtshan ma nyid// 'byung ba rnam lnga ye shes che// drug pa rdzogs pa sku gcig tu// gnas dang kha dog nyi shu lnga// rten dang grogs kyi bye brag gis// dus tshod
27a5(1): kha dog dbyibs dang brgyan// nyin dang mtshan mo'i bye brag bzhin// 'brel dang 'khril ba'i cha shas kyis// 'khor nas mya ngan 'das pa bskyed// de dag bar du rdzogs pa'i mthus/ khams gsum yul ni gsal
27a6(1): mdzad cing // gso dang sprul pa sna tshogs pas// thog ma tha ma med pa'i dbyings// zag pa med pa'i ye shes nyid// ma lus yul kun rnam dag rdzogs// de nas phyag rgya chen po'i sku// 'khor dang myang 'das
27b1(1): gnyis su med// rab tu grol ba'i bde chen mchog/ rgyal ba kun gyi ngo bo nyid// shes rab che dang thabs chen po// cha shas rdzogs pas gnyis med par// 'od gsal thig le mnyam pa'i dbyings// 'gog pa'i
27b2(1): cha shas rnam par dag/ zung du 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid do// dngos kun rang gi ngo bo las// rab tu brtags pas gzhan gnas 'joms// de dag za dad gnyis med sems// byang chub sems kyi ting nge 'dzin//
27b3(1): zhi ba chen po'i rgyal ba rnams// de dag yul bcas las 'das zhing // don 'di bstan pa'i bdag nyid kyis// phyogs dus ma lus nye bar sbyor// rang bzhin dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa dang // ye shes chen po
27b4(1): gsal 'gyur zhing // phyag rgya sngags bcas ting 'dzin gyis// bskul zhing gnas nas spyan 'dren te// dam tshig phyag rgya brtan par byed// mnyes pa'i mchod pa sna tshogs dag/ phyogs rnams kun tu rab spros te//

27b6(1): nang gsang ba'i mchod pa dang // lha mo rol bcas gnyam par sbyor// bstod tshig dbyangs kyis gsol gdab cing // dngos grub tshogs gnyis rdzogs par bskul// ye shes dkyil 'khor rdzogs byas te//

28b3(1): byed cing // yang dag myong ba chen po'i yul// don kun ston pa'i gnas rdzogs par// rab tu snyan pa'i sgra dang bcas// dri zhim yul kun gsal ba yi// myong ba'i dbang po dngos bdag nyid// gnyis 'dres
28b4(1): 'dzin par bya ba ste// de nyid phye ba las phyung ba// mi rtog bsdus pa'i ngo bo nyid// bdag po'i zhal du thim par 'gyur// shin tu bsdams pa'i rim byung ba// gsal ba'i ye shes bde ba yi// kun gsal brjod pa
28b5(1): sgra yi tshul// gnyis med thugs su shes par bya// rnam shes gsum 'das rdo rje ni// ye shes lnga rdzogs thugs nyid de// dbyings gsum yan lag 'dus ma byas// rab tu de bzhin gnas ma gyur// ma rdzogs pa

31a2(1): rnams su// dkyil 'khor bzang po brtsam pa'i phyir// phun sum tshogs pa'i gnas 'jug bya// thog mar rdo rje slob dpon bzang // sku gsung gi ni gsang ba'i bdag/ sangs rgyas theg pa kun ldan pas// snying

45b6(1): rigs kyi 'khor lo yum dang bcas// gnyis su med pa'i byin rlabs kyis// 'byung po'i tshogs rnams gshegs pa dang // spro zhing sbar dang bkod mdzad de// snga ma'i gnas kun gzhan gyur bar// bya ba chen po'i
46a1(1): / don ston mdzad// oM a hUM swA hA/ sa ma yo ga ni ra ti swA hA/ oM ma d+ha la gar+b+he hUM swa/ pra b+ha sa ma ya hUM/ oM swa shud+d+ho&haM/ oM pa ri ga ra ba ting ti hUM/ de dag yul kun bcas 'gyur te// rigs mchog phyag
46a2(1): / rgya sngags dang bcas// ting 'dzin spro ba'i tshul nyid kyis// de nyid gnas mchog 'grub par 'gyur// dpag tshad brgya dang stong la sogs// rab tu dregs pa'i khams rnams kyis// tha snyad yul rnams sbyor
46a3(1): dzad cing // 'dod pa'i dngos grub kun gyis zungs// de bzhin dri med sbyangs pa'i mthus// dpag bsam shing dang rin chen mchog/ rdzas kyi mchog rnams grub byed cing // de nas longs skrod tshim par
46a4(1): 'gyur// thun mong mngon par shes pa'i stobs// thabs kyi bye brag mtha' yas pas// rig pa'i bzang po'i phyag rgya yis// 'khor lo rnams bcas las rnams kun// ral gri mig sman bcud len
46a5(1): dang // rkang mgyog gser 'gyur bum pa bzang // mkha' 'gro 'jig rten kun spyod pa// 'khor lo la sogs rig pa'i bdag/ rdo rje a dza ri lu'i tshogs// ma g.yos kun tu khyab byed pa'i// dngos grub la
46a6(1): sogs grangs med dag/ rang gi ting 'dzin gang gis grub// dkyil 'khor kun nas dkyil 'khor ldan// 'khrul 'khor rim par sbyor ba dag/ sngags dang phyag rgyas dbang bskur te// bsam gtan yul kun
46b1(1): gsal ba la// rgyu 'bras bye brag tha dad rnams// rang gi rkyen gyis rnam par 'grub// pho brang dkyil 'khor bzang po nyid// rtse gcig mtshan mas bstan par 'gyur// oM sarba a nu ra ga ti na hUM// oM ma hA sa ma
46b2(1): ya hri/ ta ni ma na gar+b+ha hUM/ ra ga ra dza ba dza la pra mi ta na swA hA/ oM rtsa ba ga ni lo ga ni/ prad ta sha ra hUM phaT swA hA/ khams gsum thabs rnams rnam par dag/ rigs kyi 'khor lo kun rdzogs byed// yan
46b3(1): lag bden pa'i byin rlabs 'das// 'di nas las kun 'grub gyur cig/ sangs rgyas kun gyi gzi brjid dang // gsang ba'i sngags kyi 'khor lo mchog/ phyag rgya bde ba'i byin stobs kyis// las kun dngos
46b4(1): grub stobs rdzogs shing // smon lam rnam par dag pa'i rlabs// de rnams yongs su rdzogs pa yi// ji srid bdag gi dbang du ni// don bsam pa yi gnas rdzogs shing // bsnyen pa'i yan lag rnam pa zhig/ rdo

47a1(1): / pa chen po yan lag bzhis// sangs rgyas thams cad sbyor mdzad cing // rten dang brten bcas rnam par 'phrul// phyogs dus ye shes rdzogs pa'i mchog/ rab tu dag pa'i mngon sum du// thabs kyi
47a2(1): 'khor lo 'gog pa dang // shes rab phyag rgya gsang bas 'grub// gnyis med don gyis rnam par spyod// nye ba'i bstan pa'i rdzas rnams la// rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i thugs// rigs mchog phyag rgya
47a3(1): gsal 'gyur zhing // 'khrul 'khor mchog gi byin rlabs kyis// sangs rgyas stong gi gzugs ston cing // mkha' la kun gzugs snang ba yi// rdo rje 'khor lo rin chen dang // pad ma ral gri sna tshogs
47a4(1): gzugs// nges par spyod pa'i phyag rgya nyid// mtshan ma'i dngos grub sna tshogs pa// rang gi rten bzhin skye bar 'gyur// sku gsung thugs las byung ba yi// dngos grub snying po lha gnas mchog/ rang gnas mthong
47a5(1): ba'i ye shes kyis// sa gsum dbang phyug rdzogs par 'gyur// phyag rgya'i mchog gang rdzogs pa yi// lam kun bskyed pa'i yan lag ste// mi shigs dkyil 'khor sngags kyi mthus// bya ba chen po'i don rdzogs
47a6(1): shing // zag pa med pa'i dngos grub mchog/ rab tu bstan pas 'bras bu nyid// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes mchog/ dus gsum rdo rje 'dus ma byas// snang dang stong pa las grol te// mtha' dbus la sogs
47b1(1): mtha' bral zhing // gnyis med ye shes dngos grub mchog/ rig gnas byang chub sems las skyes// skye 'gag rtag chad rnams spro zhing // zhen pa'i tha snyad yul 'das shing // khyab dang khyab byed sna tshogs
47b2(1): dag/ yang dag chos kun rang bzhin las// longs spyod rdzogs dang sprul pa'i tshogs// 'bras bu mtshan bcas rnam par dag/ mi gnyis dngos grub brtan 'gyur ba'i// phyogs kun nas yang dag par bstan

53a3(1): cig sogs// bskal pa chen po'i bar du gnas// ye shes sgrib sogs kun bral zhing // ye shes phun sum tshogs pa'i bdag/ shes rab spyod pa bla na med// chos dbyings yul la mnyam par sbyor// gnyis su

53a5(1): chen por sbyor// rnam shes dbang po yul gyi rgyun// kun nas rol pa'i brtul zhugs kyis// bde ba chen po'i thig le dbyings// mtshan ma'i tshul bcas gnyis med pa'i// thabs dang shes rab 'bras bu'i
53a6(1): mchog/ kun nas dkyil 'khor snyoms 'jug cing // rang bzhin yul kun las 'das pa'i// zung 'jug gsang ba spyod pa'i mchog/ kun nas ma 'gags rol pa'i tshogs// lha dang lha mo'i dkyil 'khor
53b1(1): dbyings// rnal 'byor gnyis med spyod pa'i don// ngo mtshar yul kun rmad du byung // ji ltar 'gro nyal 'dug pa dang // spyod lam gang tshe gnas pa'i dus// sku gsung thugs kyi brtul zhugs mchog/ kun rgyud
53b2(1): rnam gsum dag pa yi// phyag rgya sngags dang ting 'dzin las// zhing khams thams cad rnam sbyangs te// yang dag bsrung ba 'grub par 'gyur// dam tshig rnam par nyam pa dang // mthu chen dbang byin brlabs
53b3(1): pa'i don// dkyil 'khor chen po brtan gnas shing // kun nas bsrung ba'i 'khor lor ldan// thabs dang shes gnas 'jug pa yi// sangs rgyas don yod grub pa'i mchog/ yang dag sbyor bas kun dgug cing //
53b4(1): ma lus 'dus pa'i thig le nyid// dam tshig chen po'i lce la bzhag/ sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma yis// rnam par gnas sbyang dbang bskur zhing // sangs rgyas kun gyis byin rlabs mchog/ kun nas 'dus pa'i
53b5(1): tshul bsgoms nas// gnas gsum rdzogs pa'i tshul 'di yis// dkyil 'khor kun nas skal ba mnyam// 'dod pa thams cad bskang ba dang // dam tshig mchog rnams rdzogs par 'gyur/ kha zas sogs kyis dub pa dang // spyi
53b6(1): bopo zla dkyil bdud rtsi lnga// yi ge lnga 'od 'bar ba'i mthus// rigs dang rigs bcas zhing khams rnams// rnam par sbyor bas rdzogs pa nyid// mtshan ma phra mo sku yi tshogs// kun nas spro zhing bsdu ba'i mthus//
54a1(1): / phyogs bcu'i rigs kyi bdag po nyid// dkyil 'khor kun gyi 'byung gnas gtso// bdud rtsi bcud rnams rab rdzogs pa'i// byang chub sems mchog snying po nyid// yang dag bsdus pas rgyas par
54a2(1): 'gyur// kun tu tshim pa'i stobs kyis ni// rdo rje 'dzin dang gral mnyam 'gyur// longs spyod 'dod kun bral ba yi// de dag rgyas par sgrub pa'i phyir// rin chen 'byung ldan ting 'dzin mchog/ rin chen bum pa
54a3(1): bzang po las// yang dag bden pa'i mthu brjod cing // ji srid me tog phreng bcas pa'i// bdud rtsi chu rgyun bzang po nyid// 'dod pa thams cad dbang mdzad pa'o// sngags dang phyag rgya rnam par
54a4(1): spel// rin chen rigs mchog thams cad kyi// byin rlabs 'od zer kun bsdus te// gnas lnga dag tu sbyor byas pas// 'khor lo'i skur rgyal gnas chen 'grub// yang dag sangs rgyas kun dang
54a5(1): mnyam// ches dbang byin rlabs nyams pa dag/ mtha' yas mgon po dpag med sku// mdzod spu rin chen gzhal yas khang // byang chub sems nyid a sha'i gzugs// 'od gsal kha dog lnga
54a6(1): dang ldan// rigs kyi phyag rgya brten byas te// chags pa'i yul bcas dbang gi sku/ khro bo mtshon chas phreng ba bcas// yang dag bsrungs pas bsrung bya ste// mi mthun las kun rnam par 'joms/ khro bo sprul pa
54b1(1): bsam yas dang // phyag rgya'i mtshan ma thams cad kyis// yul kun gnas nas shis byas te// mkha' spyod dra ba'i las chen po// rnam par sel bar dges pa dag/ sangs rgyas kun gyi mdangs dang ldan// sbrul
54b2(1): pa'i phreng ba'i 'od dang bcas// bkra shis g.yung drung dpal be'u// bum pa bzang dang gdugs kyis mtshan// mi shigs rdo rje snying po'i sku// phyag rgya bkod pa'i mtha' yas shing // tshe dbang rigs kun rgyas
54b3(1): mdzad de// yid bzhin nor bu theg pa'i mchog/ 'dod pas gnas mal thams cad du// dkyil 'khor 'brel bas chags pa'i gnas// bza' btung longs spyod thams cad la// sku gsung thugs kyi sa
54b4(1): bon gyis// 'phro 'du'i byin brlabs sprul pa'i tshogs// gnas kun nye bar sgyur byed pa'i// 'dod pa'i longs spyod lha mor bcas// sangs rgyas theg pa kun gyi bdag/ dbyings dang ye shes mnyam sbyor zhing // lnga
54b5(1): gnyis rdzogs pa'i 'od zer dang // nyi shu rtsa lnga'i 'od zer gyis// don kun gsang ba'i bdag po las// sbyor ba'i yan lag bdun snang zhing // gnyis med gnyis su sprul pa yi// rgyal ba kun 'byung bdag nyid do//

55a4(1): pa'i 'khor lo dang // rnam par sbyor ba'i byang chub sems// mtshan ldan pa yi pho brang du// bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga dang bcas// byin rlabs bsgrubs pas gsal ba nyid// bde ba chen po'i gnas rnams su// rnam par

55a6(1): dag 'gyur zhing // rnal grol dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i mchog/ ye shes tshogs mchog mtha' yas pa'i// kun tu smon lam ma 'gags pa// mtshan ma'i yul du kun byed kyang // zag bcas spyad pa brtags las

103b5(1): ni brgya yang 'tsher/ khyod kyi rdo rje the'u gshog pa g.yon pa la// las byed lha mo brgya bcu gnas// nyin bzhin rgya mtsho gting nas bzhugs pa'i tshe// klu rgyan 'bum gyis bkra shis mchod pa 'bul// mtshan zhing ri rab

104b1(1): pa'i rdo rje'i phreng ba can dang / rnal 'byor ye shes rdo rje dam tshig ma dang / mgo bo cod can legs spras rdo rje khrag 'thung dang / lag na mtshon thogs pa'i rdo rje phreng ma dang / dgra bgegs dbang du sdud
104b2(1): pa'i rdo rje'i 'khrig g.yul zlog ma dang / sbrul gyi ska rags 'ching zhing lag na mdung thung ral gri thogs ma dang / zhing lpags rked par dkris shing khrag gis myos ma dang / mig rtsa dmar por gyur pa'i rdo rje
104b3(1): 'khrugs ma dang / mtshan mo dur khrod du rgyu ba'i 'byung mo sgrol ma/ ko rlon smad dkris thod pa se ral khar thogs ma dang / mi ro rgyu ma tshems kyis 'dren pa'i rdo rje za ba mo dang / khrag gi thig les

104b5(1): drag mo chen mo dang / ma mo skrag par byed pa'i khams gsum dbang du sdud ma dang / zhing la skam par byed pa'i rdo rje kha gdong kha dang / nag mo lus mdog gnag pa'i rdo rje me stag 'phro ba mo dang / zas su khrag

109b1(1): po'i tshogs dang / rdo rje 'khor lo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje pad+ma'i tshogs dang / rdo rje khro'i tshogs dang / rdo rje mnyam par rdzogs pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje bka' nyan sprul pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje dngos grub las kyi
109b2(1): tshogs dang / rdo rje spyod pas ci las thogs pa med pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rugs su thabs mkhas pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje 'od 'phro 'bar ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje chags pa med pa'i tshul du gnas pa'i tshogs
109b3(1): dang / rdo rje sdug bsngal sel bar byed pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rigs su skyes pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje me stag phra mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje sems ma ye shes su snang ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje med pa'i tshogs dang /
109b4(1): rdo rje snyoms las med pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje sgyid lugs med pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje the tsom med pa'i sgrub pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje gsang ba'i ma tshogs dang / rdo rje rab tu dgyes mo'i tshogs dang /
109b5(1): rdo rje rol mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rnam par spros pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rgyan bkod mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje brtan mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje nam mkha' la rgyub mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje skyon dag pa mo'i tshogs dang /
109b6(1): rdo rje phyogs 'dzin pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje gdul ba la dgongs pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje brten pa'i mo tshogs dang / rdo rje tshigs mtshon pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje gab pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje sbas pa mo'i
110a1(1): tshogs dang / rdo rje thugs 'dzin pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje 'byung ba mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje shes rab 'dzin pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje bde ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rol mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje thugs kyi
110a2(1): ye shes 'dzin pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rang snang mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rang 'byung mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje kun tu mang po'i tshogs dang / rdo rje shes rab kyi pha mig dang ldan pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje kun bzang
110a3(1): longs spyod gnas pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rmongs par byed pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje sha za mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje khrag za mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje tshil za ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rkang za ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje
110a4(1): bsod nams gter 'chang ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje ye shes dkyil 'khor dang ldan pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje sgra mtha' yas pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje yon tan phrin las kyi tshogs dang / rdo rje lhun gyis grub pa'i
110a5(1): tshogs dang / rdo rje sprul pa mo'i tshogs dang / rdo rje chu las 'byung ba'i tshogs dang / rdo rje rtun bags can dang / rdo rje gdug pa gtong ba sbrul gyi chun po can dang / rdo rje 'jigs pa'i mgo brgyad pa dang / rdo rje
110a6(1): mgo sna tshogs par sprul pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje lus stong la mgo bcu pa dang / rdo rje lus brgya la mgo gcig pa'i tshogs dang / rdo rje lus sna tshogs dang / rdo rje yan lag 'bum yod pa dang / rdo rje drug pa'i
110b1(1): lag cha sna tshogs thogs pa dang / rdo rje lus brgya la mgo stong yod pa dang / rdo rje lus lnga brgya la mgo brgya pa dang / rdo rje lus bcu la mgo gcig pa dang / mgo brgyad pa la rkang pa brgyad pa dang / mgo dgu pa
110b2(1): la rkang pa gcig pa dang / de'i 'khor gyi yang sbrul gyi pho nya ni/ lcags kyi khyi ste rkang gsum po dang long brgya pa sbrel ba dang / nag po mgo dgu pa dang / shar gyi dkar mo spyan dung gi khyil mo chen dang / lho'i nag
110b3(1): mo sbrul gyi zhags pa can dang / nub kyi dmar mo zangs kyi mche ba can dang / byang gi ser mo dril bu can dang / 'di rnams kyi pho nya mo ni/ shar gyi rdo rje sder mo dang / lho'i nag mo dung gdug ma dang / nub kyi
110b4(1): dmar ser mgo can dang / byang gi ser mo las kyi bdag mo dang / rdo rje rus chen phreng ba can dang / rdo rje zangs kyi phreng ba can dang / rdo rje lcags kyi phreng ba can dang / rdo rje ral gri so can dang / rdo rje nam
110b5(1): mkha'i gung gcod ma dang / rdo rje nyi ma'i zer zhon ma dang / rdo rje chu bo'i gzhung 'dral ma dang / rdo rje rgya mtsho'i gting skrag ma dang / 'di rnams kyi sku mdog ni sna tshogs pa'o// phyag na mtshon cha sna tshogs pa'o//
110b6(1): drag byed bdag pos sgrol bar byed pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal he ru kas/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las pho nya'i las 'di gsungs so// oM hUM pho nya sum brgya drug cu yud tsam gyis ni kun
111a1(1): / 'dul zhing // yud tsam gyis ni phyogs bcur 'phro// hUM dang phaT kyi sgra sgrogs shing // bskal pa'i 'brug sgra chen po ldir// mgo gsum pa la lcags sder can// mi sha za zhing bdud dpung 'joms//
111a2(1): bltas pas bdud rnams tshig byed cing // klu yi khyim rnams rab tu 'joms// rab tu mi srun dag dang ni// 'di yang dpal gyi pho nya ste// las rnams thams cad grub par gyis/ mtshan dang dpe byad gnyis las
111a3(1): 'phro// mgyogs pa mgyogs ma'i pho nyar ldan// glog sgyu ma dang 'dra bar grags// chos nyid khyab pas mtshan ma dbyings su sdud// ye shes thugs rje 'brel bas kun la khyab/ phrin las dra bas 'gro ba rlabs kyis
111a4(1): grol// de phyir lha mo rin chen dri ba ma// oM dza la badz+ra hUM/ ye shes glog 'grus mtshan ma dbyings su gcod// skad cig thugs rjes 'khor ba dbye bsal byed// phrin las glog 'gyur 'gro ba yud kyis sgrol// dra
111a5(1): bas sdud la glog 'gyu ma yis 'dren/ badz+ra a ma ka hUM/ 'od zer dud ka 'phro ba ni// hUM dang phaT kyi sgra sgrogs shing // skal pa'i 'brug sgra chen po bzhin// kun kyang mgyogs par rlung dang mtshungs// mig gsum pa
111a6(1): la lcags sder can// mgo gsum po la rkang gsum pa// mang du za zhing bdud khyim 'joms// bltas pas bdud rnams tshig byed cing // klu yi gnas kyang nges par 'joms// 'di rnams khro bo'i pho nya ste// ha
111b1(1): ha ru lu'i sgra sgrogs shing // gang gis rlung phyogs song ba yi/ khro bo thams cad nges par 'jigs// na mo byi tsir byi/ ha ha ru lu lu b+h+yo/ mgo brgyad po la rkang brgyad po// lag pa brgyad la mig kyang brgyad// lag
111b2(1): pa brgyad ni rdo rje 'dzin// rta mgrin gnas kyang nges par 'joms// mgo drug po la rkang drug po// lag pa drug ni rgya drug gcod// rkang pa gsum ni phur bu 'dril// g.yon pa gsum ni gtor ma sbyin// gang nas
111b3(1): gang du 'gro ba'i tshe// rkang pa lcags phur rab tu drug/ 'od zer dud kas reg pi ni// tshangs pa'i gnas kyang rab tu 'jig/ lag pa g.yon pas bskyod pa ni// phra men 'khor bcas ral pa 'bar// lcags kyu
111b4(1): dgra sta rab thogs shing // zhing chen yan lag 'dzin phra 'phro// byang gi phyogs nas 'byung ba ni// lcags kyi khyi ste rkang gsum po// lcags kyi lus la nyi ma'i mig/ spu ni lcags kyu bsregs pa 'dra// bang ni glog
111b5(1): bas nges par mgyogs// skad ni 'brug pas shin tu che// rab tu mi srun 'di dag ni// phyag na rdo rje'i mthu yang 'phrog/ mgo dgu po la rkang gcig po// lus kyang gnag la 'od phyung gnag/ yan lag gnag
111b6(1): la sbrul gyis brgyan// ral pa gnag cing mche ba gnag/ mig kyang gnag la lag gnag po// mgyogs kyang rlung gis bskyod du med// 'di dag pho nya'i mchog yin pas// las rnams thams cad grub par gyis//
112a1(1): long ba brgya bsgril phyi ma na// nad mang za zhing ru lu sgrog/ mig kyang med la cang mi smra// yang na lag pa sbrel te 'gro/ 'di yang khro bo'i pho nya ste// las rnams thams cad 'grub par byed//
112a2(1): shar gyi phyogs nas 'gugs pa na// dung gi khyi mo chen mo la// dung gi ban lang sna khrid can// dung gi mi mo chen mos zhon// lag na lcags kyu 'bar ba zogs// lho yi phyogs nas 'gugs pa ni//
112a3(1): / lcags kyi khyi ste rkang gsum pa// lcags kyi spyang mo mgo dgu la// lcags kyi mi mo chen mos zhon// lag na zhags pa sgril ma thogs// nub kyi phyogs nas 'gugs pa ni// zangs kyi khyi mo chen mo la// zangs kyi
112a4(1): / mi mo chen mos zhon// lag na lcags sgrog sgril la thogs// byang gi phyogs nas 'gugs pa ni// gser gyi khyi mo chen po la// gser gyi mi mo chen mos zhon// lag na rdo rje phur bu 'dril// 'di yang dpal gyi pho

112a6(1): bzhi pa'i// dbus su bcom ldan 'das he ru ka'i// rol pa sku mdog mthing nag la// dbu gsum phyag drug pa zhig dgod// shar du rdo rje til dmar dgod/ lho ru stag gi mgo can dgod// nub tu g.yag gi mgo
112b1(1): can dgod/ byang du sbrul gyi mgo can dgod// de'i phyi rim pad+ma brgyad rim pa gsum la/ pho nya sum cu dgod/ 'dab ma gsum la/ pho nya nyi shu rtsa bzhi dgod/ de'i phyi rim snam bu la pho nya lnga bcu rtsa brgyad dgod

112b4(1): gsung dang thugs rdo rje las he ru ka'i las kyi bzlas pa 'di gsungs shing phyung ngo // bdag med gnyis rtogs sgrib pa gnyis pa spangs// thugs rjes sprul pas 'gro ba ma lus sgrol// yul med ma skyes byams

112b6(1): brda can yang dag len pa'i don go la// lha rgyud brjod pas dngos grub kun dang 'brel// bka' don gtan tshigs brjod par 'os zhes bya ba'i don to// lus gsum ngag gsum sbyin don gsum// lung gi spyi
113a1(1): gcog man ngag rdang du bya// spyi khog bcu bzhis don gyi khog phub la// bzhi bcom drug ldan rtsis bgos sa bcad de/ khro bo rtog pa mtshan ma'i gnyer gyis gshad/ 'di ni khrag 'thung ngam brjod rgyal
113a2(1): po'i lung / zhes tshig nyung zhing mdor bsdus la/ don mang por 'byung bas mdo sde zhes bya'o// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la bka' stsal pa/ lung gsum gyis sna drangs te rdeng bya'o// man ngag
113a3(1): gsum gyis mjug bsdus te blo la bzhag pa'i don to// spyi don gsum gyis lung thams cad spyi gcod do// spyi khog bcu bzhis don gyi khog dbub bo/ bdud bzhi bcom pas yon tan kun la snang ba'i che ba sgom
113a4(1): mo// rtsis mgo drug gis gcod do// khro bo rtogs pa mtshan ma'i gnyer gyis bshad pas ni/ gol sa dang ni sgrib pa spang ngo // yon tan kun rngam pas brjid pa gzhan la snang phyir rngam brjid chen po sum cu rtsa drug

113b1(1): shes rab bka' lung gsum du nges/ de la man ngag gsum na bdag tu mi rtog sprul pa mdzod nas zod/ yul du ma grub gzhon med mdzod du gshegs// yul sems gnyis med ma skyes dbyings su gcig/ nyan
113b2(1): thos rang rgyal sems tsam spong man ngag de la spyi don sum ni/ med rgyu bdag cag sgrub 'grub ltas par snang // spyod mthun khro drag bdug pa'i dpal sos 'dul// rtog 'joms sman rdzas dngos len

114b1(1): kha tar dregs pa 'joms/ de la gzugs rnam pa gnyis ni/ mi mthun nub po'i gzungs 'dra la/ a gon la ni rkang lag gdabs/ drang srong khros pa'i cha byad la/ shin tu 'khrung zhing skems bag bri/
